<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:написать.html>написать</a> (298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pisati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peyḱ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">paint</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">picture</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:написать.html>написа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to write</li></ol>

***напичкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напичкать.html>напи́чкать</a> (23947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пичкать.html>пи́чкать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">píčkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напичкать.html>напи́чкать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napíčkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пичкать.html>пи́чкать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overfeed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually forcibly or against someone's desires</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overdose, to give too much medicine to (someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stuff, to cram (someone with useless or unnecessary knowledge or information)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to oversupply (useless or unnecessary knowledge or information)</li></ol>

***наплевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наплевать.html>наплева́ть</a> (5852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плевать.html>плева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наплевать.html>наплева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naplevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to spit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spit <i>(upon)</i>, to not give a damn <i>(about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наплевать.html>наплева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>naplevátʹ</b> na éto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he doesn't care/give a damn about that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наплевать.html>наплева́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú na vsjó <b>naplevátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he doesn't care/give a damn about anything</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наплевать.html>наплева́ть</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naplevátʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">forget it!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***наплывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наплывать.html>наплыва́ть</a> (19726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наплы́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naplýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наплывать.html>наплыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naplyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наплы́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swim, to float <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, into something/someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to bump into while swimming or floating</li>
<li>to move/sweep <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, over something/someone, e.g. clouds over the sun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to accumulate while flowing, to flood <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in some amount, often a lot; of liquid or a viscous material such as mud</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to emanate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of sounds or smells</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to materialize <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of thoughts or feelings</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to form a residue</li></ol>

***напоить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напоить.html>напои́ть</a> (8662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поить.html>пои́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напоить.html>напои́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napoítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поить.html>пои́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">напа́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give to drink, to water
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напоить.html>напои́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́ем</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́м</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napoítʹ</b> kovó-libo čájem (molokóm)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give someone some tea (milk)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make drunk</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напоить.html>напои́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napoítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">напа́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffuse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напоённый.html>напоён</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аромат.html>арома́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vózdux <b>napojón</b> aromátom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the air is suffused with fragrance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наполеон.html>наполео́н</a> (6069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наполеон.html>наполео́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napoleón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наполеон.html>наполео́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наполеон.html>наполео́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наполеон.html>наполео́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of cake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a type of French howitzer made in 1853</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наползающий.html>наполза́ющий</a> (19320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наполнившийся.html>напо́лнившийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napólnivšijsja</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
